Was craving Ethiopian food and luckily we found this place nearby by searching. We were able to dine indoors and they were so friendly. We ordered the grand sampler which said it serves 2, but we hardly could finish half of it between the 2 of us! The food was great, it was a nice mix of stewed meats with lentils and other vegetables, served on top and with a side on injera. Highly recommend this place!<//Text>

<text>I like Abyssinia!  It isn't fine dining, it's a mom and pop shop.  Mom mostly runs it.  She is friendly and welcoming.

The food is delicious.  If you enjoy Ethiopian cuisine, this is the filling, satisfying family version.

Ethiopian dishes run from mild and flavorful to quite spicey and layered.  Abyssinia offers a grand sampler plate for two that will help the uninitiated experience the full spectrum.

If you're into family-run authentic cuisine, this restaurant should be on your list to try.<//text><Pics>[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipPU0azKrQrGY9lC4p4paQKxrkJIYJnUajFSXZyy=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipOIMxf603V_tVTuGyrYAx9N3bw3ekQLaSal2nuU=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]< /Pics><Resp>None<//Resp><GmapID>0x809ada4b520f6dd5:0xfe51bf7054168ff9</GmapID></record>

< Review>
Exceptional Ethiopian cuisine served in an upbeat atmosphere by a friendly, hospitable family (a little niece had just woken up from her afternoon nap near the time we were departing!) Their combination of fragrant spices and flavors is unique in comparison with other food of this type I've eaten over the years. Injera bread is promptly brought to the table, and behind through counter is an ample selection of East African herbs, seasonings and other condiments to take away to our own kitchens, though duplicating any of this restaurant's excellent recipes is futile ---- all the more reason to come again often!</Review>

<review>I've been dying to try Ethiopian food for the longest and yuuup I finally made it. I must say I have mixed emotions about this place. On one hand the flavors were great whether it be from the chicken, beef or lentils. The spiciness was perfect to me as well. The downfall to my visit was how quick the food came out. My entree of choice for a friend and I was the meal for two which included various meats and lentil in sauces as well as greens. You would think cooking all of this elaborate food would take time to come out to our table but instead came out 5-7 minutes after ordering. I'm a huge fan of made to order food and I'm going to go out on a limb and state that they don't do this technique here. Nonetheless the food was very flavorful and I enjoyed the Ethiopian cuisine.<//review><rate>3<//rate>< Pics>

Lance H.<//user_name>
<date>1550726658314</date><Resp>None</Resp><user>101479216216611316120</user>< review>
Didn't know anything about Ethiopian food. The food was wonderful. Slowly simmered stews with beef , chicken, lamb or fish (tilapia) in different sauces. I also enjoyed the collards.
My enjoyable surprise was being served family style , everything on one large platter, with the "utensils" being large crepe like bread to pick up the food.
Good friendly service, modest prices and good quantity.
Altogether an enjoyable experience to share with family or friends.< /review>

I had the giant sample platter for two as well as some of the home brewed Ethiopian Honey Wine (they actually brew their own wine so I could not pass this up). Glendale Florist exceeded my expectations- while ordering an arrangement for my grandmother's funeral, they called to make sure they had all the information they needed to coordinate with the funeral home and texted when it was delivered. When we arrived, I was floored by how beautiful the arrangement was- it was even better than the picture. They added other blooms that were beautiful (and this was with the standard order, not deluxe). My mom, who wasn't keen on getting flowers in the first place, was so thankful that we did. I also loved that they include a personalized banner with the arrangement, something that a lot of florist, especially online orders, don't include. I highly recommend Glendale Florist, and will be coming back to them when I need flowers for any occasion.</Text>

Here's why these guys rule:  I ordered flowers for my wife in the afternoon. Already a late start. The flowers I wanted were out of season, but they had some available at another store, so they got a speedy pick-up and got them for me.

My wife got her flowers and all her co-workers were impressed, and the girls were jealous... Ok, so I made up the jealous part, but she got compliments.

Highly recommend these guys.</review>

< Review>
This small coffee shop in a very quite town has not only amazing coffees and drinks but flawless customer service.

< Review>
I love this place, as a former long-term employee(5-10-18 to 5/2019 (I think the year's are right)) I can honestly say that William is a very loving and compassionate man, he's family oriented and is very positive, even when things are stressful and difficult, he keeps a smile on his face and gets what needs to be done, done. He was an amazing person to work for/with, he taught me a lot and gave me a chance to work at Rooster Wheels when I was homeless living in a van with my girlfriend at the time and our two dogs which William loved too, Breezy he says is a bunny, he really did more then a boss/coworker would ever have in any other situation, he became a really close friend of mine over the year I had been working there until my girlfriend broke up with me and I left, and quit working there, we still keep in touch from here and there, I hope this review helps some people understand that this place is simply amazing in every aspect thanks to William and his strength and will to be able to do what he does.< /Review>

< Review>
Not a bad shop at all. Repairs are solid and the price is decent but turn around time is pretty long. I have had repairs done 3 times now at this shop and it has been over two week each time. In addition, I called to check on the status of the repairs each time the bike was in the shop and told I would be called back which I wasn't.

On the plus side, the owner of the shop is extremely nice and knowledgable.

Overall, if you don't need your bike for a few weeks, this is the shop for repairs and service done at a good price. If you want a quick turn around time, I would go elsewhere.< /Review>

<userid>117158291067747928068< /userid>< Review>
They've got little boats for the peanuts now. Or maybe they just didn't have them when I last visited a year ago. The facility was clean throughout, and the staff were polite. And despite me spending over 30 mins there even after finishing my food, nobody called the cops on me.
The "all the way" hamburger I had was pretty stellar. Every bite had all the fixin's, and made good use of the foil wrapper it came in. It was a juicy and tall stack of patties on a great bun. It was however, surprisingly pricey, despite how good it was.
~$8 isn't unheard of for a good burger, but it isn't my go-to for the foundation of an economic meal. Still, if I'm ever in the area again and want a burger that will leave a lasting impression on my taste buds, I will definitely be returning.< /Review>

< Review>
Newly opened areas for foot tragic flow; gives this place a welcomed new  feel!  Sunday's only 9am 5pm

No parking. Parking lot was full. If you can find one, street parking available.

Admission...$5

The line to get in was long. However, the line moved quickly and we were in!

100 +  friendly vendors offering you the best deal they can.

Live DJ Killing it!
And Various Music playing here and there as you stroll looking for those sleepers (hidden treasure)!

Shady areas to relax/ post.

Delicious Food trucks to fuel you when you get the munchies. And yes, Rest rooms available and clean.

If you enjoy:
A lively atmosphere.
Youthful spirited energy.
Friendly faces. And a barrage of clothing, vintage items, oddities, Art,  etc.

Then I'll see you there!< /Review>

< text>
The place to find unique one-off items. From clothing and accessories to furniture and trinkets. I love wandering around the aisles, getting lost and promising myself not to spend any more money. Hard to do.

They raised entrance fee prices from $3 to $5. Cash is best to have on you for most of these merchants.

Come right when it opens to find the best items. Or if you just want to browse, take your time and get here before they close or else you‚Äôll get a million reminders on the loud speaker about closing in x-amount of minutes.

There‚Äôs a cute food court area - all located out doors. Get coffees here, rest your legs and unwind.

I love how people who shop here are wearing amazing, trendy clothes.<//text>

< review>
This is the place to go to in downtown when you don't know exactly what you want to eat or when you're with a lot of people and you can't decide where to eat. This place is packed with flavor from different parts of the world. I was able to see Thai food, Chinese food, Salvadorian food, Mexican food, Italian food, and even vegan food (yes, I know vegan food isn't a part of the world but it deserves recognition as a food category haha). < Review>
My first time at a flea market! There are two entrances ($3 each person). It's cash only, but if you don't have cash there is an ATM right by the entrance. Inside there are a lot of vintage items & stores that sell sunglasses, clothes, furniture, accessories, candles, food, & just some random items. Reminds me of an upscale outdoor swapmeet. It's only on Sunday's and it's just a fun spot to walk around! You may find a treasure or two!<//Review>

< review>
If you check the website, there's usually a coupon for $1 off entry.

Early bird def gets the worm here.  If you arrive early there's parking, but if you are like most of LA you aren't gonna get any parking, good luck with that!

As my friend says, it's like an outdoor goodwill, so you don't get the musty smells.  Are you spending an arm and leg on stuff you can get for a few dollars at Goodwill?  Probably!  But the goods are always unique and there are also almost always celebrities if that's your thing.

There is always awesome music in the food area.  And the food isn't bad either!  The guy in the corner doing corn bowls is awesome with delicious kombucha on tap.  Other notable eateries include the crepe place and there are always samples of fries.<//review>

< Text>
Its a street market showcasing local artistry and people's vintage finds. What other would call junk could also be another person's treasure. No shortage of old clothes and ornaments. There's a vendor there that has a whole department store section for aloha shirts for 7.00. Great fit for summer or for a gift for your trendy teen. It's bigger than you think so take the time to explore. Also, say hi to all the dogs you'll see. Came around 1:20, didn't find parking until 2:00 so I suggest coming early. There's also a mini street market across the street. It's a great Instagram photo spot due to the fact that there's an angel wing mural at the entrance of it. Great place to visit for 2 or so hours.< /Text>
